2026-05-10 (editor-shell sub-beta - CameraView screen->world ray contract, headless, no GPU/winit dep) - bounded single-agent substrate dispatch in A:\RCAD\RGE\. +10 net workspace tests = 7 unit tests in NEW `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs::tests` (identity_view_proj_screen_center_yields_ray_through_origin / identity_view_proj_top_left_corner_ray_origin_at_top_left_ndc / viewport_y_flip_correctness / perspective_camera_origin_at_5_screen_center_ray_through_origin / direction_is_not_normalized_per_picker_ray_contract / degenerate_zero_view_proj_returns_none / near_plane_z_is_zero_per_wgpu_convention) + 3 integration tests in NEW `crates/editor-shell/tests/camera_picker_smoke.rs` (camera_view_screen_center_picks_cuboid_top_face / camera_view_off_axis_screen_pos_misses_centered_cuboid / camera_view_composes_into_face_selection_set). The second piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter (active 2026-05-10) - turns "screen pixel + camera state -> world ray" from a pen-and-paper formula into a callable, tested, headless primitive. With sub-alpha (brep-render) + sub-beta (this dispatch) both in place, the chapter has the full headless chain: caller composes view_proj -> CameraView::screen_to_world_ray -> CadProjection::pick_face -> editor_state::FaceSelection -> EditorCoord.face_selection. **Public API**: `pub struct CameraView { pub view_proj: glam::Mat4, pub viewport_size: [f32; 2] }` + inherent method `pub fn screen_to_world_ray(&self, screen_pos: [f32; 2]) -> Option<rge_cad_projection::picking::Ray>`. The struct is `Debug + Clone + Copy`; both fields public for direct construction; method is `#[must_use]`. Re-exported at crate root as `pub use camera::CameraView`. **NDC convention LOAD-BEARING**: `view_proj` assumed wgpu/Vulkan/D3D NDC (Z in [0.0, 1.0] with 0=near and 1=far), matching `glam::Mat4::perspective_rh()` and `glam::Mat4::orthographic_rh()` (NOT the `_gl` variants which use Z in [-1.0, +1.0]). If the caller's view_proj uses GL convention, the unprojected ray will be off - caller must use a wgpu-convention projection or transform their matrix. Documented inline in the module-level docstring + verified by test 7 (`near_plane_z_is_zero_per_wgpu_convention`). **Y-flip convention**: `screen_pos` in pixels with `(0, 0)` at the top-left (winit `WindowEvent::CursorMoved` convention); NDC Y is flipped on the way in (`ndc_y = 1.0 - 2.0 * (screen_y / viewport_h)`). Verified inline by test 3 (`viewport_y_flip_correctness`). **Algorithm**: (1) screen->NDC with the Y-flip; (2) `view_proj.inverse()` with finiteness check (returns None on non-invertible / NaN-inf entries; glam returns NaN/inf for non-invertible inputs rather than `Option`); (3) construct NDC near (Z=0) + far (Z=1) clip points (wgpu convention); (4) unproject by multiplying by inverse view_proj; (5) perspective-divide on `w` (returns None if either w is exactly zero - degenerate unprojection); (6) build `Ray { origin = near, direction = far - near }`. The direction is NOT normalised per the picker's existing contract (Ray.direction need not be unit-length; the reported t is in units of direction.length()). **Substrate-honest Option<Ray> rationale**: editor-shell already operates on the "snapshot-recoverable" failure class - panicking on a degenerate camera would force the editor host to either crash or wrap every CameraView call in catch_unwind. `Option<Ray>` is the lighter contract. Callers at editor runtime are expected to supply a sane camera (the editor never constructs `Mat4::ZERO` view_proj in practice); the `None` arm is a defensive contract for the truly-degenerate case. **Layering - editor-shell is editor-tier (NOT renderer-tier)**: `forbidden-dep` rule 6 (RENDERER_CRATES `["rge-gfx", "rge-gfx-ir", "rge-brep-render"]` may not depend on game-domain crates) does NOT apply; editor-shell gains `rge-cad-projection` as a PRODUCTION dep (Tier-2 editor -> Tier-2 game-domain via the picker module's Ray re-export). `glam = "0.30"` added as production dep matching gfx's existing version specifier (no `bytemuck` feature - editor-shell never touches GPU buffers). The dispatch's stated layering decision (editor-tier -> game-domain is NOT rule 6 territory) was empirically confirmed by `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 with `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)`. **HARD NON-GOALS observed**: no `winit` event handling / `WindowEvent::CursorMoved` parsing (sub-delta); no `EditorShell::window_event` modification; no camera state tracking over time / orbit / pan / zoom / fly-cam (editor camera control is UI concern, not substrate); no view-math helpers (LookAt, perspective_rh, FOV constructors - caller composes); no `gfx::Camera` modification (renderer-tier; sub-beta stays headless); no `nalgebra` / `cgmath` / other matrix library beyond glam; no UV coords / normals helpers / tessellation-related work; no `EditorCoord` struct shape change (no new fields); no edge picking / Fillet output identity / GPU readback / new doctrine / ADR; no PLAN / IMPLEMENTATION / fileandfolderstructure / versions edits; no `panic!` / `unimplemented!` / `todo!` in production paths (Option<Ray> contract handles degeneracy explicitly); no `cargo +nightly fmt --all` cross-crate reformat (used `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-editor-shell` once mid-dispatch). **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: `crates/editor-shell/Cargo.toml` (added `rge-cad-projection = { path = "../cad-projection" }` as production dep + `glam = "0.30"` as production dep); NEW `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs` (~265L incl. 7 unit tests); `crates/editor-shell/src/lib.rs` (added `pub mod camera;` declaration + `pub use camera::CameraView;` re-export, both alphabetically; no removals); NEW `crates/editor-shell/tests/camera_picker_smoke.rs` (~210L; 3 integration tests). `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md`. **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-editor-shell --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (85 / 85; was 75; +10 net = 7 unit + 3 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2271 / 2271 pass** across 242 binaries (was 2261 / 241; +10 net workspace; +1 binary delta for the new `camera_picker_smoke.rs`; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-editor-shell` apply on two trailing-format breaks); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS - `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` with the new editor-shell -> cad-projection production dep, confirming editor-tier -> game-domain is NOT rule 6 territory; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; rollout-debt count unchanged at 30). **Public API delta** (`rge-editor-shell`): + `CameraView` struct (2 public fields: `view_proj`, `viewport_size`) + `CameraView::screen_to_world_ray` method + `pub mod camera` declaration + `pub use camera::CameraView` re-export. **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships the unproject math primitive, not interactive face picking. It does NOT wire mouse events (sub-delta), does NOT track camera state over time (sub-gamma), does NOT compute view/projection matrices (caller composes). With sub-alpha + sub-beta both in place, the chapter has the full **headless** chain: caller composes view_proj -> CameraView::screen_to_world_ray -> pick_face -> FaceSelection. Sub-gamma onwards put it on screen. **Phase 7 catalog**: still 8 operators (this dispatch operates entirely in editor-shell; cad-core source unchanged). **Workspace state**: **2271 tests / 9 enforcement + 1 supplementary lints PASS / fmt clean / 0 substantive lint exemptions / failure-class rollout-debt 30/81 (51 cleared)**.

2026-05-10 (editor-shell + rge-editor sub-delta.1.B - first triangle on screen, integration / wiring dispatch) - bounded single-agent integration dispatch in A:\RCAD\RGE\. **+5 net workspace tests** = 5 unit tests in crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs::tests for EditorCameraState (editor_camera_state_default_eye_at_3_3_3 / editor_camera_view_proj_identity_aspect_produces_finite_matrix / editor_camera_view_proj_aspect_change_affects_x_axis_only / editor_camera_to_camera_view_threads_viewport_size / editor_camera_view_proj_consistent_with_camera_view_screen_center). The fifth piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter (active 2026-05-10) — **pure integration / wiring** dispatch, no new substrate types beyond a thin CPU camera-intent holder. Composes the prior chapter primitives (RenderMesh, CameraView, render_mesh_for, SurfaceContext, LitMesh::from_render_mesh, LitMeshPipeline) into the visual moment "first triangle on screen". **Manual visual verification** (running `cargo run -p rge-editor` and inspecting that a single Lambert+Phong-shaded cuboid appears against a dark gray background) is the **load-bearing test** for this dispatch and is the **user's responsibility**; the agent did NOT run the binary because there is no display in CI. **Phase 1 — EditorCameraState struct + Default + view_proj + to_camera_view** in crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs (added alongside the existing CameraView from sub-beta; both re-exported at crate root via `pub use camera::{CameraView, EditorCameraState}`). Default places the camera at `(3, 3, 3)`, looking at the world origin with `+Y` up, `fov_y = π/4`, near 0.1, far 100.0 — three faces of a 1×1×1 cuboid at the origin (+X / +Y / +Z) are visible from this vantage point with a directional light from `(-1, -1, -1)`, producing the Lambert+Phong shading variation that visual verification looks for. `view_proj(aspect)` uses `Mat4::look_at_rh` + `Mat4::perspective_rh` (wgpu / Vulkan / D3D NDC convention LOAD-BEARING preserved per sub-beta — Z ∈ [0.0, 1.0]; NOT the `_gl` variants which use Z ∈ [-1.0, +1.0]). `to_camera_view([w, h])` composes EditorCameraState into sub-beta's CameraView for the eventual sub-delta.2 mouse-pick flow (sub-delta.1.B does not exercise it; the method is shipped together because editor-runtime camera intent and the screen-ray bridge are siblings in the same module). **Phase 2 — 13 new fields on EditorShell** in crates/editor-shell/src/lifecycle.rs (all `Option<…>` except `editor_camera`): `editor_camera: EditorCameraState`, `cad_world: Option<KernelWorld>`, `projection: Option<CadProjection>`, `cad_graph: Option<CadGraph>` (held for sub-delta.2 picker — the picker takes `&OperatorGraph` which `cad_graph.graph()` produces; pre-staging here avoids a constructor-shape change in the next dispatch — annotated `#[allow(dead_code, reason = "held for sub-δ.2 picker; not consumed in sub-δ.1.B")]`), `cad_entity: Option<KernelEntityId>`, `window: Option<Arc<Window>>`, `gfx_ctx: Option<GfxContext>`, `surface_ctx: Option<SurfaceContext>`, `pipeline: Option<LitMeshPipeline>`, `gfx_camera: Option<rge_gfx::Camera>`, `material: Option<Material>`, `light: Option<DirectionalLight>`, `cuboid_mesh: Option<LitMesh>`. All existing call sites of `EditorShell::new` / `EditorShell::with_world` see byte-identical W03 PIE behaviour: with no `cad_world` attached, `init_render_state` bails fast and the existing PlayState gating, WorldSnapshot capture/restore, AuditLedger plumbing run unchanged. **All previously-passing tests remain green** (90 / 90 in editor-shell; was 85 → +5 from EditorCameraState unit tests; rest of the editor-shell tests untouched). **Phase 3 — `EditorShell::with_world_projection_graph(cad_world: KernelWorld, projection: CadProjection, cad_graph: CadGraph) -> Self`** constructor for rge-editor's scene-load path. Captures the single `BRepHandle`-carrying entity by `world.query::<BRepHandle>().next()`; panics if zero or more-than-one match (sub-delta.1.B is single-cuboid only — multi-entity rendering is a later dispatch and the panic is the substrate-honest contract). **Phase 4 — `init_render_state(&mut self, &ActiveEventLoop)`** helper. Composes (in order): `event_loop.create_window(WindowAttributes::default().with_title("RGE Editor").with_inner_size(LogicalSize::new(1024, 768)))` → `Arc::new(window)` → `GfxContext::new_headless()` → `SurfaceContext::new(&ctx, Arc::clone(&window))` → `Camera::new(&ctx)` + `Camera::update(view_proj(initial_aspect), Mat4::IDENTITY)` → `Material::new(&ctx, &WHITE_1X1_RGBA, 1, 1)` (1×1 white texture; default phong factors `(0.1, 1.0, 0.5, 32.0)`) → `DirectionalLight::new(&ctx)` + `light.update(direction = (-1,-1,-1).normalize(), color = Vec3::ONE)` → `LitMeshPipeline::new(&ctx, camera_layout, light_layout, material_layout, surface_ctx.config().format)` (color format negotiated by surface — typically `Bgra8UnormSrgb` on Win32/Vulkan/Metal) → `projection.render_mesh_for(entity, &cad_world)` → `LitMesh::from_render_mesh(&ctx, &render_mesh)` → `window.request_redraw()` to kick off the first frame. All errors map to `String` and are logged via `tracing::error!` in `resumed`; the existing W03 ready banner still emits afterwards. **Phase 5 — `render_frame()`** helper (called from `WindowEvent::RedrawRequested`). Acquires the next surface texture via `wgpu::CurrentSurfaceTexture` enum match (wgpu 29 changed `get_current_texture` from `Result` to enum: `Success(SurfaceTexture)` / `Suboptimal(SurfaceTexture)` lift the texture; `Timeout` / `Occluded` / `Outdated` / `Lost` / `Validation` cause a `tracing::warn!` + `request_redraw` skip — verified against wgpu-29.0.3/src/api/surface_texture.rs:55). Begins a single render pass with `LoadOp::Clear(wgpu::Color { r: 0.12, g: 0.12, b: 0.14, a: 1.0 })` (dark neutral gray), `depth_stencil_attachment: None` (depth buffer AVOIDED — see Phase 7). Sets `pipeline()` + binds `Camera` at `@group(0)` + `DirectionalLight` at `@group(1)` + `Material` at `@group(2)`, sets vertex/index buffers (the cuboid mesh is always indexed per `LitMesh::from_render_mesh` → `LitMesh::from_indexed`), `draw_indexed(0..36, 0, 0..1)`. Submits, presents, schedules next redraw. **Phase 6 — `resize_render_path(new_w, new_h)`** helper (called from `WindowEvent::Resized`). Skips on `0×0` (mobile minimisation no-op); calls `surface_ctx.resize(&gfx_ctx, w, h)` to reconfigure; recomputes `view_proj` from the new aspect ratio and uploads to the camera UBO via `Camera::update`. **Phase 7 — Depth buffer status: AVOIDED** (preferred per dispatch spec). The existing `LitMeshPipeline::new` declares `depth_stencil: None`; sub-delta.1.B preserves that. For a single Lambert+Phong-shaded cuboid: back-face triangles compute Lambert dot ≤ 0 (the directional light from `(-1,-1,-1)` lights the +X / +Y / +Z faces; the −X / −Y / −Z faces fall to ambient-only ≈ `(0.1, 0.1, 0.1) × white` per the default phong factors), and the camera at `(3, 3, 3)` looking at origin has the front-facing triangles drawn over the back-facing ones in submission order. **No `gfx` modification was required** — staying within the strict "no gfx modification" non-goal. **Phase 8 — `editor/rge-editor/src/main.rs` full rewrite** (from 5-line stub to ~85L). Builds the cuboid scene from scratch using the same construction pattern as `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_picking_smoke.rs` and `crates/editor-shell/tests/camera_picker_smoke.rs`: `CadGraph::new()` → `begin_operation()` → `add_operator(OperatorNode::Cuboid(CuboidOp { width: 1.0, height: 1.0, depth: 1.0 }))` → `set_root(...)` → `commit("rge-editor demo cuboid")` → `CadProjection::new()` → `World::new()` → `world.register_snapshot_component::<BRepHandle>()` → `projection.spawn_brep_entity(&mut world, cuboid_node)` → mutate `BRepHandle.brep_owner = Some(BRepOwnerId::from_bytes([0x42; 16]))` → `projection.tick(&mut world, &graph, Tolerance::new(0.001).expect("tol"))` → `EditorShell::with_world_projection_graph(world, projection, graph)` → `EventLoop::new().run_app(&mut shell)`. Uses `tracing_subscriber::fmt::try_init()` (best-effort; wrapped in `drop(...)` per clippy `let_underscore_drop`). `ExitCode::SUCCESS` on clean exit; `ExitCode::FAILURE` on `run_app` error. **Layering verification (rule-6-checked)**: editor-shell is editor-tier (NOT in `RENDERER_CRATES`), so `forbidden-dep` rule 6 (RENDERER_CRATES → game-domain forbidden) does NOT fire; editor → renderer is permitted. 4 new dep edges on editor-shell (`rge-gfx` + `rge-brep-render` + `wgpu` production deps; `rge-cad-core` promoted from dev-dep to production for the `CadGraph` ownership in `with_world_projection_graph`'s signature) and 6 deps on rge-editor (`rge-editor-shell` + `rge-cad-core` + `rge-cad-projection` + `rge-kernel-ecs` + `winit` + `tracing-subscriber`). All pass `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)`. The dispatch's PRECONDITION step (run lint check BEFORE writing impl) confirmed this empirically; if the lint had fired, the dispatch would have stopped and reported back rather than writing impl code. **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance): no `gfx` source modification (depth buffer was avoided → no `LitMeshPipeline` change required);
